add_namespace = abyssinia
add_namespace = abyssinia_news

news_event = {
	id = abyssinia_news.1
	immediate = {log = "[Root.GetName]: event abyssinia_news.1"}#Auto-logging
	title = abyssinia_news.1.t
	desc = abyssinia_news.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_pony_diplomacy
	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = abyssinia_news.1.a
		trigger = {
			tag = MDL
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = abyssinia_news.1.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = ABY
				original_tag = MGY
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = abyssinia_news.1.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = MDL
				original_tag = ABY
				original_tag = MGY
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Starting event
	id = abyssinia.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event abyssinia.1"}
	title = abyssinia.1.t
	desc = abyssinia.1.d
	picture = GFX_event_stormlands_portrait
	timeout_days = 6
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = katztime }
	}

	option = {
		name = abyssinia.1.a
		
		country_event = abyssinia.2
	}
}

country_event = { #Third event wow these comments are very detailed and insightful
	id = abyssinia.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event abyssinia.3"}
	title = abyssinia.3.t
	desc = abyssinia.3.d
	picture = GFX_event_zebrica_1
	timeout_days = 6
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = abyssinia.3.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = abyssinia.4 days = 4 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = ABY_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
					has_country_flag = ABY_AI_HISTORICAL
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = ABY_ai_behavior
						option = ABY_HISTORICAL
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = abyssinia.3.b
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = abyssinia.5 days = 8 }
			country_event = { id = abyssinia.4 days = 4 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = ABY_AI_COMMUNIST
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = ABY_ai_behavior
						option = ABY_COMMUNIST_ALTERNATE
					}
					has_country_flag = ABY_AI_FASCIST
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = ABY_ai_behavior
						option = ABY_FASCIST_ALTERNATE
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = abyssinia.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event abyssinia.8"}
	title = abyssinia.8.t
	desc = abyssinia.8.d
	picture = GFX_event_green_mountain
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ABY_its_joever
			has_country_flag = ABY_maybe_its_joever
		}
	}
	timeout_days = 6
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = abyssinia.8.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ABY_king_absent
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ABY_king_absent
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = abyssinia.14 days = 8 }
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

			}

		}
	}

			limit = {
				has_character = ABY_donkey_general
			}
			ABY_donkey_general = {
				retire = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = abyssinia.198.b
		add_political_power = 25
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ANS = {
					exists = yes
				}
				ASS = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ASS = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = ABY_donkey_general
					}
					ABY_donkey_general = {
						set_nationality = ASS 
					}
				}
			}
			ASS = {
				country_event = abyssinia.199
			}
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = ABY_donkey_general
					}
					ABY_donkey_general = {
						set_nationality = ANS 
					}
				}
			}
			ANS = {
				country_event = abyssinia.199
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = abyssinia.198.c
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}

			limit = {

			}
			country_event = abyssinia.208
			ROOT = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = PREV modifier = common_cause }

					amount = 1500
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
		}
	}
	option = { #Nows our chance

			has_government = fascism
			owns_state = 1200
			NOT = {
				owns_state = 1201
			}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event abyssinia.214"}
	title = {
		text = abyssinia.214.t_clawomon
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				has_idea = ABY_monsoc_morticia
				has_idea = ABY_monsoc_gomez
			}
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = abyssinia.214.t_no_clawomon
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = ABY_monsoc_morticia
				has_idea = ABY_monsoc_gomez
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = abyssinia.214.d_first_citizen
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader_with_trait = ABY_first_citizen
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = abyssinia.214.d_chief_minister
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader_with_trait = ABY_chief_minister
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = abyssinia.214.d_empress
		trigger = { 
			has_country_leader_with_trait = ABY_empress_of_abyssinians
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_event_zebrica_1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = abyssinia.214.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = -0.05 }
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = abyssinia.215 days = 15 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #ABY offers alliance to MDL
	id = abyssinia.217
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event abyssinia.217"}
	title = abyssinia.217.t
	desc = abyssinia.217.d
	picture = GFX_event_zebrica_1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = abyssinia.217.a
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				owns_state = 741
				owns_state = 738
				owns_state = 740
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = abyssinia.218 days = 3 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = abyssinia.217.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				owns_state = 741
				owns_state = 738
				owns_state = 740
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = abyssinia.219 days = 3 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = abyssinia.217.c
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = abyssinia.220 days = 3 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = democratic
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Manedalusia agrees
	id = abyssinia.218
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event abyssinia.218"}
	title = abyssinia.218.t
	desc = abyssinia.218.d
	picture = GFX_event_zebrica_1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = abyssinia.218.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					country_event = generic.2
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_faction = ABY_COM_ALLIANCE
				#Unfortunately i have to copy the code twice so the tooltip generates properly
				FROM = {
					country_event = generic.5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = generic.5
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Manedalusia agrees on one condition
	id = abyssinia.219
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event abyssinia.219"}
	title = abyssinia.219.t
	desc = abyssinia.219.d
	picture = GFX_event_zebrica_1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = abyssinia.219.a
		set_country_flag = ABY_agreed_to_liberate_mdl
		unlock_decision_tooltip = ABY_ally_with_mdl
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 741
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					741 = {
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				remove_state_claim = 741
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					741 = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				remove_state_core = 741
			}
			MDL = {
				transfer_state = 741
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						owns_state = 741
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = { 
				type = take_state_focus
				target = 741.owner
				generator = { 741 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 740
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					740 = {
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				remove_state_claim = 740
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					740 = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				remove_state_core = 740
			}
			MDL = {
				transfer_state = 740
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						owns_state = 740
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = { 
				type = take_state_focus
				target = 740.owner
				generator = { 740 }
			}
		}
		if = {

			}
			if = {
				limit = {

						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				remove_state_claim = 738
			}
			if = {

					}
				}
				remove_state_core = 738
			}

			}
		}

				FROM = {
					NOT = {

					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = { 
				type = take_state_focus
				target = 738.owner
				generator = { 738 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 764

					}

country_event = { #Multiracial Empire/Union
	id = abyssinia.234
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event abyssinia.234"}

	desc = abyssinia.234.d
	picture = GFX_event_feast
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = abyssinia.234.a
		add_political_power = 300
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.05 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = ABY_first_citizen
			}
			swap_ruler_traits = { remove = ABY_first_citizen add = ABY_first_citizen_2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = ABY_empress_of_abyssinians
			}
			swap_ruler_traits = { remove = ABY_empress_of_abyssinians add = ABY_empress_of_liberty }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = ABY_monsoc_cosmetic
					has_cosmetic_tag = ABY_empire_2
				}
			}
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			set_cosmetic_tag = ABY_liberty_empire
		}
		else = {
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			set_cosmetic_tag = ABY_five_race_union
		}
	}
}
